[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | //@ts-nocheck
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | import { parseJWT } from '@redwoodjs/api'
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | import { AuthenticationError, ForbiddenError } from '@redwoodjs/graphql-server'
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | import { logger } from 'src/lib/logger'
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | /**
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * getCurrentUser returns the user information together with
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * an optional collection of roles used by requireAuth() to check
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * if the user is authenticated or has role-based access
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @param decoded - The decoded access token containing user info and JWT claims like `sub`. Note could be null.
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @param { token, SupportedAuthTypes type } - The access token itself as well as the auth provider type
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @param { APIGatewayEvent event, Context context } - An object which contains information from the invoker
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * such as headers and cookies, and the context information about the invocation such as IP Address
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @see https://github.com/redwoodjs/redwood/tree/main/packages/auth for examples
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | export const getCurrentUser = async (
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   decoded,
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   /* eslint-disable-next-line no-unused-vars, @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   { token, type },
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   /* eslint-disable-next-line no-unused-vars, @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   { event, context }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | ) => {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   if (!decoded) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     logger.warn('Missing decoded user')
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     return null
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   const { roles } = parseJWT({ decoded })
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   const { privateMetadata, ...userWithoutPrivateMetadata } = decoded
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   if (roles) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     return {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       roles,
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       ...userWithoutPrivateMetadata,
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     };
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   return {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     ...userWithoutPrivateMetadata,
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   };
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | /**
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * The user is authenticated if there is a currentUser in the context
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @returns {boolean} - If the currentUser is authenticated
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | export const isAuthenticated = () => {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   return !!context.currentUser
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | /**
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * When checking role membership, roles can be a single value, a list, or none.
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * You can use Prisma enums too (if you're using them for roles), just import your enum type from `@prisma/client`
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | type AllowedRoles = string | string[] | undefined
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | /**
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * When checking role membership, roles can be a single value, a list, or none.
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * You can use Prisma enums too (if you're using them for roles), just import your enum type from `@prisma/client`
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | /**
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * Checks if the currentUser is authenticated (and assigned one of the given roles)
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @param roles: {@link AllowedRoles} - Checks if the currentUser is assigned one of these roles
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @returns {boolean} - Returns true if the currentUser is logged in and assigned one of the given roles,
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * or when no roles are provided to check against. Otherwise returns false.
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | export const hasRole = (roles: AllowedRoles): boolean => {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   if (!isAuthenticated()) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     return false
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   const currentUserRoles = context.currentUser?.roles
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   if (typeof roles === 'string') {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     if (typeof currentUserRoles === 'string') {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       // roles to check is a string, currentUser.roles is a string
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       return currentUserRoles === roles
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     } else if (Array.isArray(currentUserRoles)) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       // roles to check is a string, currentUser.roles is an array
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       return currentUserRoles?.some((allowedRole) => roles === allowedRole)
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   if (Array.isArray(roles)) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     if (Array.isArray(currentUserRoles)) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       // roles to check is an array, currentUser.roles is an array
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       return currentUserRoles?.some((allowedRole) =>
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |         roles.includes(allowedRole)
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       )
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     } else if (typeof currentUserRoles === 'string') {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       // roles to check is an array, currentUser.roles is a string
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |       return roles.some((allowedRole) => currentUserRoles === allowedRole)
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   // roles not found
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   return false
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | /**
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * Use requireAuth in your services to check that a user is logged in,
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * whether or not they are assigned a role, and optionally raise an
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * error if they're not.
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @param roles: {@link AllowedRoles} - When checking role membership, these roles grant access.
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @returns - If the currentUser is authenticated (and assigned one of the given roles)
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @throws {@link AuthenticationError} - If the currentUser is not authenticated
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @throws {@link ForbiddenError} If the currentUser is not allowed due to role permissions
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  *
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  * @see https://github.com/redwoodjs/redwood/tree/main/packages/auth for examples
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |  */
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | export const requireAuth = ({ roles }: { roles?: AllowedRoles } = {}) => {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   if (!isAuthenticated()) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     throw new AuthenticationError("You don't have permission to do that.")
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | 
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   if (roles && !hasRole(roles)) {
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |     throw new ForbiddenError("You don't have access to do that.")
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   |   }
[⚙️ CI/🧪 Test       ]   | }
